document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  if (!e.target.closest('.om-nav-dropdown')) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.om-dropdown-menu').forEach(m => m.classList.remove('open'));
  }
});

/* â”€â”€ STRAND / TOPIC STRUCTURE â”€â”€ */
const QG_STRANDS = [
  { id: 'number', name: 'Number', dotColor: '#1c75bc', subsections: [
      { label: 'Factors, multiples and prime numbers', topics: ['Factors', 'Multiples', 'Prime numbers', 'Product of prime factors', 'Lowest common multiple', 'Highest common factor'] },
      { label: 'Fractions', topics: ['Simplify fractions', 'Fraction of a number', 'Add and subtract fractions', 'Multiply fractions', 'Divide fractions', 'Mixed numbers and all operations', 'Recurring decimals to fractions'] },
      { label: 'Indices', topics: ['Basic laws of indices', 'Harder laws of indices', 'Fractional and negative indices'] },
      { label: 'Negatives', topics: ['Add and subtract negatives', 'Multiply and divide negatives'] },
      { label: 'Operations', topics: ['Multiply by 10, 100 and 1000', 'Divide by 10, 100 and 1000', 'Short multiplication', 'Short division', 'Long multiplication', 'Long division', 'BIDMAS'] },
      { label: 'Percentages', topics: ['Common percentages of numbers', 'Percentages of numbers', 'Increase/decrease by a percentage', 'Percentage change', 'Simple interest', 'Compound interest'] },
      { label: 'Ratio', topics: ['Simplify a ratio', 'Split into a ratio', 'Direct proportion', 'Inverse proportion'] },
      { label: 'Standard form', topics: ['Ordinary number to standard form', 'Standard form to ordinary number'] }
  ]},
  { id: 'algebra', name: 'Algebra', dotColor: '#009444', subsections: [
      { label: 'Expanding', topics: ['Expand single brackets', 'Expand double brackets', 'Expand triple brackets'] },
      { label: 'Factorising', topics: ['Factorise into single brackets', 'Factorise quadratics'] },
      { label: 'Inequalities', topics: ['Integer solutions to an inequality', 'Solve one-step inequalities', 'Solve multistep inequalities'] },
      { label: 'Quadratics', topics: ['Complete the square', 'Factorise harder quadratics', 'Solve quadratics', 'Quadratic formula'] },
      { label: 'Sequences', topics: ['nth term', 'Finding terms', 'Numbers in sequences', 'Quadratic nth term'] },
      { label: 'Simplifying', topics: ['Collecting like terms'] },
      { label: 'Solving equations', topics: ['Solve one-step equations', 'Solve two-step equations', 'Solve equations with brackets', 'Solve equations with unknown on both sides', 'Simultaneous equations'] },
      { label: 'Substitution', topics: ['Basic substitution', 'Harder substitution'] }
  ]},
  { id: 'statistics', name: 'Statistics', dotColor: '#800080', subsections: [
      { label: 'Averages', topics: ['Mean', 'Median', 'Mode', 'Range'] }
  ]},
  { id: 'geometry', name: 'Geometry', dotColor: '#f7941e', subsections: [
      { label: 'Area', topics: ['Area of a square', 'Area of a rectangle', 'Area of a triangle', 'Area of a parallelogram', 'Area of a trapezium', 'Area of a kite', 'Area of compound shapes'] },

      { label: 'Circles', topics: ['Area of a circle', 'Circumference of a circle'] }

];

function qgAllTopics(strand) {
  return strand.subsections.flatMap(s => s.topics);
}

// Master list of every topic in the order it appears on the page (strand by strand, subsection by subsection)
const QG_PAGE_ORDER = QG_STRANDS.flatMap(strand => qgAllTopics(strand));

function qgSelectedInPageOrder() {
  return QG_PAGE_ORDER.filter(topic => qgSelected.has(topic));
}

let qgSelected = new Set();

function qgChipId(topic) { return 'qg-chip-' + topic.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '-'); }

function qgBuildStrands() {
  const container = document.getElementById('qg-strands');
  container.innerHTML = QG_STRANDS.map(strand => `
    <div class="qg-strand" id="qg-strand-${strand.id}">
      <div class="qg-strand-header">
        <span class="qg-strand-name"><span class="qg-strand-dot" style="background:${strand.dotColor}"></span>${strand.name}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="qg-strand-body">
        ${strand.subsections.map(sub => `
          <div>
            ${sub.label ? `<div class="qg-subsection-label">${sub.label}</div>` : ''}
            <div class="qg-chip-row">
              ${sub.topics.map(t => `<button class="qg-chip ${strand.id}" id="${qgChipId(t)}" onclick="qgToggleChip('${t.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">${t}</button>`).join('')}
            </div>
          </div>`).join('')}
      </div>
    </div>`).join('');
  qgUpdateSummary();
}

function qgToggleChip(topic) {
  const btn = document.getElementById(qgChipId(topic));
  if (qgSelected.has(topic)) { qgSelected.delete(topic); btn.classList.remove('selected'); }
  else { qgSelected.add(topic); btn.classList.add('selected'); }
  qgUpdateSummary();
}

document.getElementById('qg-qcount').addEventListener('change', qgUpdateSummary);

function qgUpdateSummary() {
  const n = qgSelected.size;
  const qcount = parseInt(document.getElementById('qg-qcount').value);
  const total = n * qcount;
  document.getElementById('qg-summary').textContent = n === 0
    ? 'No topics selected'
    : n + ' topic' + (n > 1 ? 's' : '') + ' selected, ' + total + ' question' + (total > 1 ? 's' : '') + ' total';
}

function qgShuffle(arr) {
  const a = arr.slice();
  for (let i = a.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
    const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
    [a[i], a[j]] = [a[j], a[i]];
  }
  return a;
}

function qgEsc(str) {
  return String(str).replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
}

/* Converts plain-text maths notation into rendered HTML:
   - "x^2" or "2^3" -> superscript powers
   - "3/4" -> stacked fraction (only for digit/digit, so x/4 style division stays inline)
   - "{12x^7y^3/6x^3y}" -> always-stacked fraction, for algebraic/indices terms (curly braces opt in explicitly)
   - "^(1/2)" or "^(-1/2)" -> superscript exponent containing a stacked fraction, for fractional/negative indices
   - "[4]" -> dot above that digit, for recurring decimals
   - "Prefix: eq1~~eq2" -> two-line layout, eq2 aligned under eq1 rather than under the prefix (e.g. simultaneous equations)
   Escaping happens first, then notation is layered on top. */
function qgFormatInline(str) {
  let s = qgEsc(str);

  // Explicit stacked fraction: {numerator/denominator}, for terms too complex for the plain digit/digit rule below
  s = s.replace(/\{([^{}\/]+)\/([^{}]+)\}/g, function(m, num, den) {
    return '<span class="qg-frac"><span class="qg-frac-num">' + num.trim() + '</span><span class="qg-frac-den">' + den.trim() + '</span></span>';
  });

  // Fractional / negative fractional exponents: base^(content) -> superscript, stacking a plain fraction inside if present
  s = s.replace(/\^\(([^)]+)\)/g, function(m, content) {
    let inner = content.trim().replace(/(-?\d+)\/(\d+)/g, '<span class="qg-frac"><span class="qg-frac-num">$1</span><span class="qg-frac-den">$2</span></span>');
    return '<sup>' + inner + '</sup>';
  });

  // Stacked fractions: whole-number numerator/denominator only (avoids breaking Ã· expressions or algebra/x)
  s = s.replace(/(\d+)\/(\d+)/g, '<span class="qg-frac"><span class="qg-frac-num">$1</span><span class="qg-frac-den">$2</span></span>');

  // Recurring decimal dot: [4] -> dot above that digit
  s = s.replace(/\[(\d)\]/g, '<span class="qg-dot">$1</span>');

  // Powers: base^exponent, base can be a letter/number/closing bracket, exponent can be a number or short letter term
  s = s.replace(/([a-zA-Z0-9\)])\^(-?\d+|[a-zA-Z])/g, '$1<sup>$2</sup>');

  // Algebraic x: render as italic serif x
  s = s.replace(/(?<![a-wyz])x(?![a-wyz])/g, '<em class="qg-x">x</em>');

  // Litres/millilitres: render l/ml with the curly script l
  s = s.replace(/(?<=\d ?)ml\b/g, 'm<span class="qg-l">â„“</span>');
  s = s.replace(/(?<=\d )l\b/g, '<span class="qg-l">â„“</span>');

  // Thousands separator: any whole-number run of 4+ digits (not a decimal's fractional part) gets commas
  s = s.replace(/(?<!\.)\b\d{4,}\b/g, m => Number(m).toLocaleString('en-GB'));

  return s;
}

function qgFormatMaths(str) {
  // Two-line layout: "Prefix: eq1~~eq2" -> eq2 sits on its own line, aligned under eq1
  let twoLine = String(str).match(/^([^:]+:\s+)([^~]+)~~(.+)$/);
  if (twoLine) {
    let prefix = qgEsc(twoLine[1]);
    let eq1 = qgFormatInline(twoLine[2]);
    let eq2 = qgFormatInline(twoLine[3]);
    return '<span style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;"><span>' + prefix + eq1 + '</span><span><span style="visibility:hidden">' + prefix + '</span>' + eq2 + '</span></span>';
  }
  return qgFormatInline(str);
}

function qgGenerate() {
  if (qgSelected.size === 0) { alert('Please select at least one topic.'); return; }

  const qcount = parseInt(document.getElementById('qg-qcount').value);
  const topicStrandMap = {};
  QG_STRANDS.forEach(strand => qgAllTopics(strand).forEach(t => { topicStrandMap[t] = strand; }));

  let html = `
    <div class="qg-out-header">
      <span class="qg-out-title">Generated questions</span>
      <div class="qg-out-actions">
        <button class="qg-btn-outline" id="qg-toggle-all-btn" onclick="qgToggleAllAnswers()">Show all answers</button>
        <button class="qg-btn-outline" onclick="qgClear()">Clear questions</button>
        <button class="btn btn-green" onclick="qgPrint(false)">Print worksheet</button>
        <button class="btn btn-blue" onclick="qgPrint(true)">Print with working space</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;

  let answerListHtml = '';
  let n = 0;
  qgSelectedInPageOrder().forEach(topic => {
    const strand = topicStrandMap[topic];
    const bank = QG_BANK[topic] || [];
    const picked = qgShuffle(bank).slice(0, Math.min(qcount, bank.length));

    html += `<div class="qg-topic-block"><span class="qg-topic-label" style="background:${strand.dotColor}">${topic}</span><div class="qg-q-list">`;
    answerListHtml += `<div class="qg-ans-topic"><span class="qg-ans-topic-label" style="background:${strand.dotColor}">${topic}</span><div class="qg-ans-page-list">`;

    picked.forEach(item => {
      n++;
      const uid = 'qg-ans-' + n;
      const diagHtml = item.diagram ? `<div class="qg-diagram">${item.diagram}</div>` : '';
      html += `<div class="qg-q-item">
        <span class="qg-q-num">${n}.</span>
        <div class="qg-q-main">
          <span class="qg-q-text">${qgFormatMaths(item.q)}</span>
          ${diagHtml}
          <span class="qg-answer" id="${uid}">${qgFormatMaths(item.a)}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="qg-q-right">
          <button class="qg-show-btn" onclick="qgToggleAnswer('${uid}', this)">Show answer</button>
        </div>
        <div class="qg-working-space"></div>
      </div>`;

      answerListHtml += `<div class="qg-ans-page-row">
        <span class="qg-ans-page-num">${n}.</span>
        <span class="qg-ans-page-text">${qgFormatMaths(item.a)}</span>
      </div>`;
    });

    html += `</div></div>`;
    answerListHtml += `</div></div>`;
  });

  html += `<div class="qg-answer-page">
    <h2 class="qg-answer-page-title">Answers</h2>
    ${answerListHtml}
  </div>`;

  const out = document.getElementById('qg-output');
  out.innerHTML = html;
  out.style.display = 'block';
  out.classList.remove('qg-print-working');
  out.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
}

function qgClear() {
  const out = document.getElementById('qg-output');
  out.innerHTML = '';
  out.style.display = 'none';

  qgSelected.forEach(topic => {
    const btn = document.getElementById(qgChipId(topic));
    if (btn) btn.classList.remove('selected');
  });
  qgSelected.clear();
  qgUpdateSummary();

  document.querySelector('.qg-controls').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
}

function qgPrint(withWorking) {
  const out = document.getElementById('qg-output');
  out.classList.toggle('qg-print-working', withWorking);
  requestAnimationFrame(() => {
    requestAnimationFrame(() => window.print());
  });
}

function qgToggleAnswer(uid, btn) {
  const visible = document.getElementById(uid).classList.toggle('vis');
  btn.textContent = visible ? 'Hide answer' : 'Show answer';
  qgSyncToggleAllLabel();
}

function qgToggleAllAnswers() {
  const answers = document.querySelectorAll('.qg-answer');
  const allVisible = Array.from(answers).every(e => e.classList.contains('vis'));
  answers.forEach(e => e.classList.toggle('vis', !allVisible));
  document.querySelectorAll('.qg-show-btn').forEach(b => b.textContent = allVisible ? 'Show answer' : 'Hide answer');
  qgSyncToggleAllLabel(!allVisible);
}

function qgSyncToggleAllLabel(forceState) {
  const btn = document.getElementById('qg-toggle-all-btn');
  if (!btn) return;
  const answers = document.querySelectorAll('.qg-answer');
  const allVisible = forceState !== undefined ? forceState : (answers.length > 0 && Array.from(answers).every(e => e.classList.contains('vis')));
  btn.textContent = allVisible ? 'Hide all answers' : 'Show all answers';
}

qgBuildStrands();

</script>
